Feature preprocessing\n        def compute_features(raw_data):\n            features = []\n            # VIX features\n            features.append(np.log(raw_data['vix']))\n            features.append(np.diff(raw_data['vix']))\n            \n            # Yield curve\n            features.append(raw_data['yield_2_10'])\n            \n            # Credit spreads\n            features.append(np.log(raw_data['credit_spreads']))\n            \n            # Volatility regime indicators\n            features.append(raw_data['volatility_regime'])\n            \n            # Factor valuation spreads\n            features.append(raw_data['value_momentum_spread'])\n            \n            return np.array(features).T\n        \n        # Compute features and standardize\n        processed_features = compute_features(data)\n        return self.scaler.fit_transform(processed_features)\n    \n    def detect_regimes(self, data):\n        # Prepare features\n        X = self.prepare_features(data)\n        \n        # HMM Model\n        model = hmm.GaussianHMM(\n            n_components=self.n_regimes, \n            covariance_type='full',\n            n_iter=100\n        )\n        \n        # Fit model\n        model.fit(X)\n        \n        # Predict regimes\n        hidden_states = model.predict(X)\n        \n        return {\n            'regimes': hidden_states,\n            'regime_probabilities': model.predict_proba(X)\n        }\n    \n    def analyze_regime_characteristics(self, data, regimes):\n        # Detailed regime analysis\n        regime_stats = {}\n        for regime in range(self.n_regimes):\n            regime_mask = (regimes == regime)\n            regime_stats[regime] = {\n                'mean': np.mean(data[regime_mask], axis=0),\n                'volatility': np.std(data[regime_mask], axis=0)\n            }\n        return regime_stats\n\n# Usage example\ndef factor_timing_strategy(data):\n    detector = FactorRegimeDetector(n_regimes=3, lookback=180)\n    regime_analysis = detector.detect_regimes(data)\n    \n    # Dynamic factor allocation\n    current_regime = regime_analysis['regimes'][-1]\n    allocation_map = {\n        0: {'value': 0.7, 'momentum': 0.3},  # Conservative regime\n        1: {'value': 0.3, 'momentum': 0.7},  # Momentum regime\n        2: {'value': 0.5, 'momentum': 0.5}   # Balanced regime\n    }\n    \n    return allocation_map[current_regime]\n```\n\nKey Recommendations:\n1.
